*Date: 2006-07-30*

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 16: Chinese Grand Prix
*Date: 2006-10-01*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |
